_webdebugger.py 
1    # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
2    # flake8: noqa
3    
4    import threading
5    import json
6    from gc import get_objects, garbage
7    from kivy.clock import Clock
8    from kivy.cache import Cache
9    from collections import OrderedDict
10   from kivy.logger import Logger
11   
12   try:
13       from flask import Flask, render_template_string, make_response
14   except ImportError:
15       Logger.error('WebDebugger: unable to import Flask. Install it!')
16       raise
17   
18   history_max = 250
19   
20   
21   class MissingOrderedDict(OrderedDict):
22   
23       def __missing__(self, key):
24           self[key] = [0] * history_max
25           return self[key]
26   
27   
28   metrics = MissingOrderedDict()
29   app = Flask(__name__)
30   
31   
32   @app.route('/')
33   def index():
34       return render_template_string(html_index)
35   
36   
37   @app.route('/metrics.json')
38   def metrics_json():
39       resp = make_response(json.dumps(metrics), 200)
40       resp.headers['Content-Type'] = 'text/json'
41       return resp
42   
43   
44   @app.route('/f/<name>')
45   def getfile(name):
46       name = name.replace('.', '_')
47       text = globals()[name]
48       resp = make_response(text, 200)
49       if name.endswith('_js'):
50           resp.headers['Content-Type'] = 'text/javascript'
51       elif name.endswith('_jpg'):
52           resp.headers['Content-Type'] = 'image/jpeg'
53       return resp
54   
55   
56   class FlaskThread(threading.Thread):
57   
58       def run(self):
59           Clock.schedule_interval(self.dump_metrics, .1)
60           app.run(debug=True, use_debugger=True, use_reloader=False)
61   
62       def dump_metrics(self, dt):
63           m = metrics
64           m['Python objects'].append(len(get_objects()))
65           m['Python garbage'].append(len(garbage))
66           m['FPS (internal)'].append(Clock.get_fps())
67           m['FPS (real)'].append(Clock.get_rfps())
68           m['Events'].append(len(Clock.get_events()))
69           for category in Cache._categories:
70               m['Cache ' + category].append(
71                   len(Cache._objects.get(category, [])))
72           for values in m.values():
73               values.pop(0)
74               values[0] = 0
75   
76   
77   def start(win, ctx):
78       ctx.thread = FlaskThread()
79       ctx.thread.daemon = True
80       ctx.thread.start()
81   
82   
83   def stop(win, ctx):
84       pass
85   
86   # -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
87   # DATA FILES
88   # -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
89   
90   
91   html_index = ''' 
92   <html> 
93   <head> 
94   <title>Kivy - Web Debugger</title> 
95   <script type='text/javascript' src='/f/jquery.js'></script> 
96   <script type='text/javascript' src='/f/raphael.js'></script> 
97   <script type='text/javascript' src='/f/g_raphael.js'></script> 
98   <script type='text/javascript' src='/f/g_raphael_line.js'></script> 
99   <style type='text/css'> 
100  body { 
101      font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; 
102      font-size: 13px; 
103      color: #eee; 
104      background: url('/f/background.jpg') repeat-x #718693; 
105  } 
106   
107  .panel { 
108      width: 400px; 
109      float: left; 
110      background-color: #BCCAD5; 
111      margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px; 
112      padding: 20px; 
113      -moz-border-radius: 16px; 
114      -webkit-border-radius: 16px; 
115      border-radius: 16px; 
116  } 
117   
118  .panel h2 { 
119      margin: 0px; 
120      padding: 0px 0px 10px 0px; 
121      color: #516673; 
122  } 
123   
124  </style> 
125  <script type='text/javascript'> 
126   
127  var graphics = {}; 
128  var rid = 0; 
129  var ids = {} 
130   
131  function request_metrics() { 
132      $.ajax({ 
133      url: '/metrics.json', 
134      error: function(xhr, status) { 
135          $('#error').html('Connection lost').show(); 
136          setTimeout('request_metrics()', 1000); 
137      }, 
138      success: function(data) { 
139          $('#error').hide(); 
140          for (var key in data) { 
141              if ( typeof(graphics[key]) == 'undefined' ) { 
142                  rid += 1; 
143                  $('<div class="panel panel' + rid + '"><div id="r' + rid + '"></div></div>').appendTo($('#metrics')); 
144                  $('.panel' + rid).prepend( 
145                      $('<h2 id="h' + rid + '"></h2>').html(key)); 
146                  graphics[key] = Raphael('r' + rid, 400, 150); 
147                  ids[key] = rid; 
148              } 
149   
150              var indices = []; 
151              for (var i = 0; i < data[key].length; i++) 
152                  indices[i] = i; 
153              var r = graphics[key]; 
154              $('#h'+ids[key]).html(key + ': ' + data[key][i-1]); 
155              r.clear(); 
156              r.linechart(26, 0, 340, 150, indices, data[key], { 
157                  shade: true, axis: "0 1 0 1" }); 
158          } 
159          setTimeout('request_metrics()', 250); 
160      } 
161      }); 
162  } 
163   
164  request_metrics(); 
165   
166  </script> 
167  </head> 
168  <body> 
169  <h1>Kivy - Web Debugger</h1> 
170  <div id='error'></div> 
171   
172  <h2>Metrics</h2> 
173  <div id='metrics'> 
174  </div> 
175  </body> 
176  </html> 
177  '''
